Meanwhile /blogs/b2b-ppc/ owns the bare 'b2b ppc' query at position 15.6. Two pages cannot both be the 'b2b ppc' target. → Re-target this page to a how-to head term it actually earns, e.g. primary 'how to run b2b ppc campaigns' (or 'b2b ppc campaigns'), and let /blogs/b2b-ppc/ keep the bare 'b2b ppc' primary. Differentiate the angles explicitly or consolidate the two into one guide.

- ⚠️ cannibalization benign vs /glossary/what-is-ppc/ (low, none) — Glossary definition page picking up 2 impressions at pos 73.5 — pure noise. Different (definitional) intent, no real ranking split.

It gets effectively no traction for its actual legaltech-SaaS target, and the queries it does surface for are a different audience (law firms/attorneys, not legaltech software vendors). → Decide which intent the page serves. Keep the legaltech-SaaS focus and strengthen on-page legaltech-software signals (CLM, e-discovery, legal-ops buyer language) so it stops being interpreted as a law-firm marketing page; do not chase the attorney/lawyer-SEO queries here. If law-firm marketing is a wanted target, that belongs on a separate page rather than diluting this one.

- ⚠️ keyword [primary_mismatch]: Editorial primary is the bare term 'saas ppc', but this is a commercial agency landing page (title 'B2B SaaS PPC Agency'). GSC shows it actually draws on agency-intent queries: 'saas ppc agency' (514 impr, the dominant query), 'b2b saas ppc agency' (153), 'saas ppc advertising company' (85), with 'saas ppc' itself only 130. The bare term 'saas ppc' is also the editorial primary of the blog /blogs/saas-ppc/, so the landing page is mis-aimed at an informational blog's target. → Retarget this landing page's primary to 'saas ppc agency' (matches its title and dominant GSC demand) and leave 'saas ppc' to the /blogs/saas-ppc/ post.
- ⚠️ cannibalization ✅real vs /saas-ppc/faqs/ (medium, canonical) — This is a child FAQ subpage of the same landing page ranking for the parent's own 'saas ppc' demand (25 impr, pos 81; plus another row). Same intent, same page family splitting signals - consolidate or canonicalize the FAQ subpage to the parent.
- ⚠️ cannibalization benign vs /blogs/best-saas-ppc-agencies/ (low, monitor) — Comparison blog ('best saas ppc agencies') vs the service landing page; different intent. (Note: this landing page's own primary should be 'saas ppc agency' per the keyword finding, but the comparison listicle is still a distinct intent.)
- ⚠️ cannibalization benign vs /list/best-saas-ppc-agencies/ (low, monitor) — Comparison listicle (primary 'best saas ppc agencies') vs the service landing page; different intent, both legitimate.
